It is served on the same origin as the API, so no second port or reverse proxy is needed. Pass ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--no-web"}]," for an API-only daemon."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"One agent process, many clients"}]," — under the default ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"sessionScope: 'single'"}],", every client connecting to the daemon shares one ACP session. Live cross-client collaboration on the same conversation, the same file diffs, the same permission prompts."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Reconnect-safe streaming"}]," — SSE with ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Last-Event-ID"}]," reconnect lets a client drop and pick up exactly where it left off (within the ring’s replay window)."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"First-responder permissions"}]," — when the agent asks for permission to run a tool, every connected client sees the request; whichever client answers first wins."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"One daemon, one workspace"}]," — each ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen serve"}]," process binds to exactly one workspace at boot (per ",["$","$L1c",null,{"href":"https://github.com/QwenLM/qwen-code/issues/3803","children":"#3803"}]," §02). Multi-workspace deployments run one daemon per workspace on separate ports (or behind an orchestrator)."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Remote runtime control"}]," (",["$","$L1c",null,{"href":"https://github.com/QwenLM/qwen-code/issues/4175","children":"#4175"}]," PR 17) — change a session’s approval mode (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /session/:id/approval-mode"}],"), toggle a tool per workspace (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /workspace/tools/:name/enable"}],"), scaffold an empty ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"QWEN.md"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /workspace/init"}],", mechanical only — does NOT call the model; for AI-fill, follow up with ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /session/:id/prompt"}],"), restart a single MCP server with a budget pre-check (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /workspace/mcp/:server/restart"}],"), or add/remove MCP servers at runtime without a daemon restart (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /workspace/mcp/servers"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"DELETE /workspace/mcp/servers/:name"}],"). All strict-gated — configure ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--token"}]," first."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Session recap"}]," (",["$","$L1c",null,{"href":"https://github.com/QwenLM/qwen-code/issues/4175","children":"#4175"}]," follow-up) — fetch a one-sentence “where did I leave off” summary of an active session (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /session/:id/recap"}],"). Wraps core’s ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"generateSessionRecap"}]," as a side-query against the fast model; pollutes neither the main chat history nor the SSE stream. Non-strict gate (same posture as ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"/prompt"}],"); SDK helper ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"client.recapSession(sessionId)"}],".\n",["$","ul",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-[.75em] x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:list-disc x:ms-[1.5em]","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Known limit — token-cost amplification:"}]," the route is a pure-cost endpoint (each call is an LLM side-query, no state benefit) and the daemon has no per-route rate limit in v1. On a no-token loopback default a buggy or malicious local client can spam it to burn tokens. Configure ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--token"}]," (and optionally ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--require-auth"}],") on shared dev hosts before exposing the daemon."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Concurrent recap safety:"}]," two simultaneous ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"/recap"}]," calls on the same session run two independent side-queries. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"generateSessionRecap"}]," reads a snapshot of the chat history via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"GeminiClient.getChat().getHistory()"}]," and feeds it to a separate ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"BaseLlmClient.generateText"}]," call (via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"runSideQuery"}],"); it never appends to or mutates the session’s ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"GeminiChat"}],". Safe to call from multiple clients without coordination."]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","h2",null,{"id":"v016-alpha-known-limits","className":"x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-10 x:border-b x:pb-1 x:text-3xl nextra-border","children":["v0.16-alpha known limits",["$","$L1d",null,{"id":"v016-alpha-known-limits"}]]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["The first npm release of ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen serve"}]," (v0.16-alpha) is intentionally narrow — text-only chat / coding for developers running the daemon on their own machine. 'authorized'"}]}]]}]]}]]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"The daemon never opens a browser on your behalf."}]," Even when running locally, the daemon stays passive — it returns the URL and lets the SDK / user choose where to open it. This is intentional: a daemon on a headless pod that called ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"xdg-open"}]," would silently fail, masking the actual auth surface. Mirror ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"gh auth login"}],"’s “Press Enter to open browser” UX in your client."]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--require-auth"}]," and dev convenience."]}]," The device-flow routes use the strict mutation gate (PR 15), which means a token-less loopback default returns ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"401 token_required"}],". Locally, the simplest way around this during development is ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen serve --token=dev-token"}],"; you don’t need ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--require-auth"}]," unless you’re hardening the loopback default."]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Cross-daemon limitation."}]," ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"oauth_creds.json"}]," is daemon-shared (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"~/.qwen/oauth_creds.json"}],"), so a successful login in daemon A is automatically picked up by daemon B’s next token refresh — but daemon B’s SDK clients won’t receive the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"auth_device_flow_authorized"}]," event (events are per-daemon)."]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Cross-client take-over."}]," Two SDK clients on the same daemon that both ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"POST /workspace/auth/device-flow"}]," for the same provider get the per-provider singleton: the first call starts a fresh IdP request and returns ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"attached: false"}],"; the second call returns the EXISTING in-flight entry with ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"attached: true"}],".
